### [112] [Simorgh at SemEval-2026 task 7: Region-Aware Hybrid Retrieval for Low-Resource Cultural Reasoning in Multilingual Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27636)
*Hadi Bayrami Asl Tekanlou,Mahdi Bakhtiyarzadeh,Jafar Razmara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型在低资源语言的文化知识问答中的表现，并提出了一种结合区域特征的混合检索机制，有效提升了多语言、多文化领域问题的答案相关性，但训练数据不足的问题仍未完全解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在通用领域表现优异，但在数字资源稀缺语言的文化相关知识推理上存在不足，因此需要改进其跨语言、跨文化的问答能力。

Method: 构建了涵盖30种语言及多种社会文化领域（如美食、体育、家庭等）的BLEnD数据集；提出了结合BM25（词法匹配）和稠密语义检索、并引入区域权重的混合检索方法；最后利用检索文档构建结构化提示，结合Qwen3-14B量化模型进行确定性选项选择。

Result: 实验表明，混合检索方法相较单纯参数推断能提升模型在多语言文化问题上的稳定性和性能，但数据较少语言与数据丰富语言之间依然存在显著性能差距。

Conclusion: 区域感知混合检索能一定程度提升大模型的跨语言文化问答能力，但由于训练数据不均衡，完全弥补稀缺语言差距仍有挑战。

Abstract: Although Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate excellent capabilities and performance for general reasoning tasks within the general public domain, they may face challenges with culturally grounded knowledge within languages with limited digital and textual data. In this paper, we investigate culturally grounded multiple-choice question answering with the BLEnD benchmark, which consists of a multilingual corpus of 30 languages and covers various socio-cultural domains, such as cuisine, sports, family, etc. We propose a region-aware hybrid retrieval approach that combines BM25 lexical matching and dense semantic similarity with regional weighting heuristics to improve the relevance of the answer. The retrieved documents are used to construct a structured prompt for the Qwen3-14B quantized model with logit-based deterministic answer selection. The experimental results show improvements to cross-lingual stability with the hybrid retrieval approach over pure parametric inference for culturally grounded question answering. However, there are still notable performance gaps between languages with more and less training data. This shows that the limitations of the retrieval augmentation approach are not entirely overcome by the training data imbalance problem.

</details>


### [113] [Learning to Translate from Soft to Hard LLM Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27642)
*Pitipat Kongsomjit,Suryansh Goyal,Jacob Whitehill*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出通过训练专用的软提示-自然语言翻译模型，提升大语言模型（LLMs）在特定任务中的翻译质量，并增强软提示的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前软提示调优虽可高效适配大模型，但其可解释性较差，限制了实际应用和理解。针对这一问题，作者希望探索提升软提示可解释性的方法，并克服现有训练免费（training-free）方法在翻译任务中的局限。

Method: 作者基于最近的可解释化软提示工作，训练了专门的软提示-自然语言翻译模型，并在多个数据集集合（DoDs）上进行了定量和定性比较，与现有方法（如InSPEcT）进行对比。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的翻译器在流畅度和准确性方面均优于现有训练免调方法。此外，相比原始软提示和部分小样本学习方法，优化后的软提示可通过文本翻译迁移至更大闭源API模型上，表现更佳。

Conclusion: 本工作不仅提升了软提示的可解释性，还展示了其在跨模型迁移和下游应用中的巨大潜力，为软提示在实际应用中广泛部署奠定了基础。

Abstract: Soft prompt tuning is a parameter-efficient method for adapting LLMs to specific tasks, but suffers from a lack of interpretability. Building on recent work on interpreting soft prompts (Ramati et al., 2024), we explore how training a dedicated soft prompt to natural language translation model can yield higher translation quality. In particular, in both quantitative and qualitative comparisons on multiple Datasets of Datasets (DoDs), we demonstrate that our translator produces fluent, accurate verbalizations that outperforms existing training-free methods like InSPEcT. In addition to advancing interpretability, our work suggests a promising downstream application: soft prompts optimized on small, open-source models can be translated into portable text prompts that, when deployed on larger closed-API models, exceed the performance of the original soft prompt and, in some cases, even few-shot learning.

### [114] [Disentangling Language Roles in Multilingual LLM Task Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27649)
*Qishi Zhan,Minxuan Hu,Seoyeon Jang,Lei Zhao,Ziheng Chen,Man Liang,Xinyue Xiang,Jiaxin Liu,Guansu Wang,Liang He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了MTM-Bench，一个专门评估多语种大模型（Multilingual LLM）在指令、内容和回复三种语言角色交错情况下的能力基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多语种大模型经常在任务中出现指令语言、内容语言和回复语言不一致的情况，但现有基准很少将三种语言角色完全交错、独立评估其影响。因此迫切需要一个全交叉、细致分解影响因素的基准来研究多语种指令跟随任务中的性能瓶颈。

Method: 作者提出MTM-Bench，设计为(L_instr, L_content, L_resp)三元组，在中英文、西班牙语三种语言下，穷举27种组合，涵盖2430个实例，包括语义反转、终态抽取和语言纯粹性等任务。对20个主流及开源大模型从语义正确性、目标语言满足、约束达成、其他语言污染率、联合成功率等多维度进行量化评分，并通过人工审核验证分数。

Result: 采用完全交叉设计后发现，性能下降并不仅与语言不匹配数量相关，而是高度依赖于每种语言在任务结构中扮演的角色。回复语言是决定表现的主导因素，仅回复语言不匹配即可导致显著降低。模型在不同任务和不匹配场景下表现排序不同，表现下降的通道多样，说明现有评估（如语义准确率）难以刻画多语种任务的真实可靠性。

Conclusion: 多语种任务评估应全面考察各种语言角色的交互，尤其要关注回复语言的作用。单纯依赖匹配数量或语义准确率不足以全面评估大模型的多语种能力。MTM-Bench为多语种LLM可靠性检验提供了更细腻、系统的度量方式，对今后相关模型和基准的设计有重要启示。

Abstract: Multilingual LLMs are increasingly used when instruction, source content, and required response languages do not coincide. Existing benchmarks have expanded multilingual instruction-following evaluation, but they rarely isolate these three roles within a fully crossed design. We introduce MTM-Bench, a controlled benchmark for language-conditioned task execution in which each instance is defined by a triplet \((L_{\text{instr}}, L_{\text{content}}, L_{\text{resp}})\). Across English, Spanish, and Chinese, MTM-Bench enumerates all 27 triplets and contains 2{,}430 instances per model across semantic reversal, final-state extraction, and language purity with update realization. We evaluate 20 frontier and open-weight LLMs using decomposed metrics for semantic correctness, target-language adherence, constraint satisfaction, contamination ratio, and joint success, with scoring validated by a targeted human audit. The fully crossed design reveals that degradation is organized by the role a language occupies in the task structure, not merely by mismatch count. The response-language role is the dominant axis of variation, and a single response-slot mismatch accounts for most degradation. The response-only and full-mismatch comparison suggests that mismatch count is not a monotonic predictor of difficulty, with model-level ordering varying across systems. Task families fail through distinct channels, showing that semantic correctness alone does not capture reliable multilingual task execution.

</details>


### [115] [TRACES: Proactive Safety Auditing for Multi-Turn LLM Agents via Trajectory-State Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27690)
*Jiaqian Li,Yanshu Li,Boxuan Zhang,Ruixiang Tang,Kuan-Hao Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种主动审计方法TRACES，可以在LLM智能体多轮工具使用和环境交互过程中，基于隐藏表示预测中间步骤中的风险，而非仅在最终结果后进行反应性检查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的LLM安检主要依赖于最终结果的反应性审计，无法及时发现和阻止早期出现的安全风险。因此，作者希望设计一种可以提前预警、在中间步骤就能够辨识风险的机制。

Method: 作者提出TRACES方法，从LLM隐藏表征中学习轨迹前缀（partial trajectory）级别的风险状态，通过诱导机制特征、建模其随时间变化，实现对智能体行为风险航迹的预测。训练时不依赖昂贵且模糊的逐步风险标注，仅用弱的轨迹级监督，输出细粒度的前缀风险估计。

Result: TRACES在多个智能体安全基准任务上，提升了完整轨迹的安全性预测和前瞻性风险辨识能力。分析表明，该方法得到的风险状态还能用于训练更安全的智能体。

Conclusion: 主动式审计（如TRACES）可以识别和预警LLM智能体在复杂任务中长程演化的潜在风险，有助于预防安全事件，并为构建更安全的智能体提供了新的思路。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly operate through multi-turn tool use and environment interaction, where safety risks often emerge from intermediate steps long before they surface in the final outcome. Reactive auditing is therefore insufficient: post-hoc diagnosis frequently misses the chance to flag risks while they are unfolding. We propose TRACES, a representation-based proactive auditor that learns prefix-level trajectory risk states from the hidden representations of an observer LLM. TRACES induces latent mechanism features from step representations and models their temporal evolution to estimate whether a partial trajectory is drifting toward unsafe behavior. To sidestep the cost and ambiguity of step-level risk annotation, TRACES is trained with weak trajectory-level supervision while still producing dense prefix-level risk estimates. Across multiple agent safety benchmarks, TRACES improves both full-trajectory safety prediction and proactive risk discrimination. Our analyses further suggest that these risk states can help train a safer agent, highlighting the broader potential of proactive auditing for long-horizon agent safety.

</details>


### [116] [ReverseMath: Answer Inversion for Scalable and Verifiable Mathematical Problem Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27709)
*Raoyuan Zhao,Yihong Liu,Yupei Du,Hinrich Schütze,Michael A. Hedderich*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ReverseMath提出了一种通过答案反转生成新的数学题目方法，用于评估和训练大语言模型（LLM），提升模型推理能力并检测记忆倾向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数学推理基准多已公开并被反复训练和评测，无法有效区分模型的真实推理能力与记忆能力，而人工构建新题目成本高，造成评估和训练方式受限。

Method: ReverseMath方法：给定数学题及其答案，先掩盖原题中的一个数值，以原答案为已知条件，重构题目使被掩盖数值成为新答案，从而生成结构合法且答案已知的新题。该方法既可用于生成评估题目，也可用作RL训练自动标注数据扩充。

Result: 1）评测中，模型在反转题目上的行为显著变化，部分模型无法解答反转题，甚至输出原答案，反映出一定的记忆效应。2）训练中，加入ReverseMath生成的样本作为增强，能提升模型在多数学推理基准上的表现。

Conclusion: ReverseMath能高效生成可验证的新数学题目，为大模型推理评测和训练提供便利，是一种有效的分析工具和数据生成方法。

Abstract: Mathematical reasoning benchmarks are vital for evaluating large language models (LLMs), but many are static and repeatedly exposed through public evaluation and training pipelines, making it difficult to separate genuine reasoning from memorization. Meanwhile, manually constructing new math problems with reliable answers remains costly. We introduce ReverseMath, a scalable method for generating new math problems through answer inversion. Given a problem and its answer, ReverseMath masks a numerical value in the original problem, treats the original answer as a known condition, and rewrites the problem so that the masked value becomes the new answer. The generated problem reverses the original input-output relation, making its answer known by construction. We study ReverseMath for both evaluation and training. For evaluation, paired original/reversed problems reveal substantial behavioral shifts: models sometimes fail on reversed problems and even incorrectly output the original answer, suggesting memorization-like behavior. For training, ReverseMath provides automatically labeled reversed problems as data augmentation for reinforcement learning (RL). Experiments show that including ReverseMath-generated data improves mathematical reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks, demonstrating its value as both an analysis tool and a scalable source of verifiable training data.

</details>


### [117] [UserHarness: Harnessing User Minds for Stronger Agent Theory-of-Mind](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27721)
*Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为UserHarness的新方法，将用户理论（ToM）推理转变为对用户心理状态的显式重建，旨在提升智能助手对用户意图和信念的理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的ToM评估方法多采用复杂流程，且仅间接建模用户行为，未能直接重建用户的心理状态，忽略了信念-意图-行为这一核心结构，从而影响推理性能。

Method: UserHarness将ToM推理问题分解为用户心理状态的组成部分，包括用户与外部环境的关系及其后续行为。该方法显式追踪用户观察到的信息、形成的信念、意图以及行动，帮助智能体更清晰地理解和预测用户行为。

Result: 在五个基准测试中，UserHarness的宏观准确率高达95.94%，比现有推断方法提升超过15%，比最强的纯提示方法提升约20%。

Conclusion: 结果表明，精准的用户理解需从用户心理根源出发。UserHarness为构建更具适应性的未来智能助手奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Understanding what a user believes and intends is central to building effective agent assistants. This ability is often evaluated through Theory-of-Mind (ToM) tasks, where success requires reasoning from the user's perspective. However, many existing approaches address ToM with complex pipelines that model behavior indirectly, without explicitly reconstructing the user's mental state. This misses the core structure of the problem: users act based on their beliefs, which are updated through observations of the environment; beliefs and intentions jointly determine actions, which in turn change the environment; and social reasoning often requires nested beliefs about what others believe or intend. We propose UserHarness, a simple framework that reframes ToM reasoning as explicit user-mind reconstruction. UserHarness decomposes the user's mental state, its relation to the external environment, and the actions that follow from it, enabling agents to track what the user observes, believes, intends, and does. Across five benchmarks, UserHarness reaches up to 95.94% macro accuracy, improving over existing inference methods by more than 15% relative and over the strongest prompt-only harness by about 20% relative. These results suggest that robust user understanding requires reasoning from the roots of the user's mind, positioning user harnessing as a promising foundation for more adaptive future assistants.

</details>


### [118] [Escape the Language Prior: Mitigating Late-Stage Modality Collapse in Audio Reasoning via Modality-Aware Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27741)
*Cihan Xiao,Yiwen Shao,Chenxing Li,Xiang He,Zhenwen Liang,Steve Yves,Sanjeev Khudanpur,Liefeng Bo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对多模态大模型（如音频和多模态语言模型）在强化学习后训练中，容易出现模态塌缩、推断偏离原始模态信号的问题，提出了新的解决方案MAPO，显著提升了多模态推理表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大语言模型在推理过程中，常因标准强化学习方法忽视模态对非文本信息的依赖，导致模型逐渐偏向文本先验，丧失对主导源信号（如音频）的准确利用，产生虚假、自信但不真实的回答（即“模态塌缩”）。

Method: 作者提出了MODALITY-AWARE POLICY OPTIMIZATION（MAPO）框架。其核心包括两点：（1）应用基于跨模态差分熵的模态相关性掩码策略，动态聚焦于模态关键Token的策略梯度；（2）引入辅助注意力损失分支，对内部注意分布采取目标化、时序性缩放的惩罚，促进推理过程中保持模态对齐和有效信号利用。

Result: 在复杂音频推理基准测试中，MAPO方法显著提升了多模态模型的长链推理准确率和执行复杂指令的能力，并在若干主要开放权重基准上刷新了性能记录。

Conclusion: MAPO方法无需依赖领域特定的归纳偏置，只用原生统计信号即可有效缓解多种多模态系统中的“认知塌缩”问题，为未来多模态智能体的健壮推理提供了新方向。

Abstract: Audio and omni-modal large language models exhibit impressive cross-modal reasoning capabilities. However, applying standard reinforcement learning post-training algorithms to these models exposes a critical structural vulnerability: methods like GRPO apply uniform policy gradients across all tokens, ignoring their unequal dependence on the non-text source modality. This exacerbates late-stage modality collapse during extended chain-of-thought generation, where models progressively abandon the primary source signal in favor of compressed textual priors, leading to confident but ungrounded hallucinations. To address this, we introduce Modality-Aware Policy Optimization (MAPO), a novel dual-branch reinforcement learning framework. First, MAPO dynamically concentrates the policy gradient on modality-critical tokens using a modality relevance mask, which is derived from the cross-modal differential entropy between an audio-ablated reference and the multimodal policy. Second, it integrates an auxiliary attention loss branch that applies a targeted, temporally scaled penalty to the model's internal attention distributions. This ensures the model actively sustains cross-modal grounding deep into the reasoning trace. Evaluations on complex audio reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that MAPO substantially improves long-horizon reasoning fidelity and multimodal instruction following, achieving highly competitive performance and setting new state-of-the-art results on several key benchmarks among open-weight models. By relying strictly on native statistical signals rather than domain-specific inductive biases, MAPO offers a promising foundation for mitigating epistemic collapse across diverse multimodal systems.

</details>


### [119] [ChildEval: When large language models meet children's personalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27805)
*Yanyan Luo,Xue Han,Chunxu Zhao,Ruiqiao Bai,Yaxing Zhang,Qian Hu,Lijun Mei,Junlan Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了ChildEval基准，用于系统性评估大语言模型（LLM）在儿童定制化偏好理解与对话中的能力，并通过实验验证了微调对提升表现的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型多被用于个性化聊天机器人，但其对儿童、尤其是对3-6岁儿童偏好的理解和跟随能力尚缺乏系统性评估。为了弥补这一空白，需要有面向儿童的专门评估基准。

Method: 作者构建了ChildEval基准，包含29K个3-6岁儿童的人设档案（静态背景信息）与相关偏好描述（显性/隐性，体现在独句或6-10轮对话中），并覆盖了5个主类、14个子类的日常与发育领域。提出了精细化、以儿童为中心的评估方案，并将其用于评测开源LLM及微调对表现的影响。

Result: 实验显示，不同个性化表现方式对LLM回应有显著影响，基于ChildEval的微调可有效提升模型在儿童场景下的偏好理解和跟随能力。

Conclusion: ChildEval为后续LLM在儿童领域的研究与实际应用提供了初步、系统的评估和改进路径，验证了面向儿童个性化微调的重要性。

Abstract: While LLMs enable personalized chatbots, their effectiveness in child-centered personalization remains unclear, as systematic evaluation of child-specific preferences is still lacking. To address this gap, we introduce ChildEval, a benchmark for evaluating LLMs' ability to infer and follow child-centered preferences in long-context conversations. ChildEval contains 29K synthesized persona profiles of children aged 3-6, providing relatively static background information. Each persona is associated with a child preference-which may align with, conflict with, or be independent of the persona-expressed either explicitly in a single sentence or implicitly through 6-10 turn dialogues. Explicit and implicit preferences are designed to reflect the same underlying preference but differ in expression, capturing dynamic aspects of preference expression rather than changes in the static persona. The benchmark spans five top-level and fourteen sub-level categories covering children's daily lives and development. We further propose fine-grained, child-centric evaluation protocols to systematically assess open-source LLMs. Experimental results demonstrate how different personalized representations affect LLM responses and suggest that finetuning on ChildEval can enhance child-centered performance. Our code and dataset are available at https://github.com/ziyanluo/ChildEval.

</details>


### [120] [DecomposeRL: Learning to Ask Useful, Informative, and Diverse Questions for Semi-Supervised, Traceable Claim Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27858)
*Shubhashis Roy Dipta,Ankur Padia,Francis Ferraro*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DecomposeRL的主张验证方法，兼顾高准确率和可解释性，有效提升了当前主张验证的性能和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有主张验证方法在准确性与可解释性之间存在权衡。端到端分类器虽然准确，但缺乏可追溯性；分解式方法可生成可检查的推理链条，但在基准测试集上性能不佳。作者希望兼顾两者优势。

Method: DecomposeRL将主张分解建模为强化学习策略，通过GRPO训练并采用多奖励机制，既支持全监督也支持半监督学习。同时，提出数据筛选流程，从11.5万条样本中提炼出信号密集的5000条训练，显著降低GRPO训练成本。

Result: 在仅用约5000条精炼训练数据下，DecomposeRL-7B在11个领域（含生物医学、政治、科学及通用领域）基准测试上获得86.3%的域内和69.8%的跨域平衡准确率。模型参数量仅为对标模型的1/4，但表现可比32B模型和GPT-4.1-mini，在仅10%标注数据下半监督设定更是超越现有基线。

Conclusion: DecomposeRL成功结合了性能与可解释性，降低了训练成本，是高效、可解释主张验证的有力方案，对实际应用具有重要价值。

Abstract: Claim verification splits between end-to-end classifiers that are accurate but yields no inspectable traces, and decomposition-based methods produce inspectable traces but lag performance on benchmark datasets. We propose DecomposeRL an accurate claim-verifier that produce inspectable traces. DecomposeRL frames decomposition as an RL policy trained with GRPO and a multi-faceted reward ensemble, enabling both fully supervised and semi-supervised learning from unlabeled claims. DecomposeRL addresses the prohibitive training cost of GRPO with a data-curation funnel that distills 115K fact-verification claims into a compact, learning-signal-dense subset of 5K claims. We show that a DecomposeRL-7B policy trained with full supervision on only ~5K curated claims achieves 86.3 in-domain and 69.8 out-of-domain balanced accuracy across 11 claim-verification benchmarks containing biomedical, political, scientific, and general-domain claims. Despite being 4x smaller, it matches 32B baselines and GPT-4.1-mini, and it further outperforms baselines in a semi-supervised setting with only 10% labeled claims data. Code, data, and models are available at https://dipta007.github.io/DecomposeRL

</details>


### [121] [GRADE: Generalizable Reasoning-Aware Dialogue Evaluation for AI Tutors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27866)
*Parth Bhalerao,Jeromy Chang,David Chou,Oana Ignat*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文系统性地评估了开源大语言模型在学生-导师对话场景中的教学能力，提出了GRADE方法，实验表明合适的模型和微调方案可达到甚至超越商用方案的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI导师不仅需输出事实正确答案，还要能发现学生错误、定位问题、给出引导和可操作建议。现有评估方法和模型多关注单一能力，缺乏系统性、多维度的教学能力评估框架。

Method: 作者构建了GRADE评测体系，基于BEA 2025 TutorMind数据集，分析5个主流开源大模型，包括零样本推理、LoRA微调、合成数据增强、链式推理（CoT+Reasoning）、单任务与多任务设置，并对比不同模型与pipeline在各类场景下的表现。

Result: Gemma3-12B在单任务场景下表现最优，Gemma3-27B（8位精度）多任务预测更可靠。数据增强有助于低效模型提升，链式推理对合成数据生成更有利。微调（LoRA）在结构化分类目标下可能影响模型守规能力。不同模型和推理方式对碳排放影响明显。

Conclusion: 精心选择和设计的开源LoRA微调方案能在关键教学维度上媲美甚至超越商用或集成系统。GRADE为AI导师教学能力评测提供了系统框架与开源数据代码，有望促进相关领域发展。

Abstract: Evaluating AI tutor responses requires more than factual correctness: tutors must identify mistakes, locate errors, provide guidance, and offer actionable next steps. We present GRADE, a systematic study of open-source models for pedagogical ability assessment in student-tutor dialogues. Building on the BEA 2025 TutorMind setting, we evaluate 120 configurations across five language models, zero-shot inference, LoRA fine-tuning, synthetic augmentation, CoT+Reasoning, and single-task versus multitask formulations. Gemma3-12B performs best for single-task evaluation, while Gemma3-27B in 8-bit precision is more reliable for multitask prediction. We find that augmentation helps models that struggle with the original data, verification adds limited gains despite higher cost, and CoT+Reasoning is more useful for synthetic data generation than direct classification. We further show that LoRA fine-tuning on structured classification objectives interferes with instruction-following behavior under thinking mode, redirecting generation away from the required evaluation format. Carbon analysis shows that model choice and reasoning mode substantially affect emissions. Overall, GRADE shows that carefully selected open-source LoRA pipelines can match or surpass proprietary and ensemble-based systems on key pedagogical dimensions, with code and data available at https://github.com/pvbgeek/GRADE.

### [122] [Syllabic-Structure Decoder for Automatic Speech Recognition in Vietnamese](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27874)
*Nghia Hieu Nguyen,Quan Ngoc Hoang,Long Hoang Huu Nguyen,Kiet Van Nguyen,Ngan Luu-Thuy Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于音节结构解码器的越南语自动语音识别(ASR)方法，用更紧凑的音素级别建模替代传统的字符或词级别预测，在标准与多方言语音数据集上均优于现有主流模型，并且词汇量更小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ASR系统通常以字符、子词或词为单位进行预测，但这种方式未显式反映语音的音系结构且词表庞大。在越南语中，音节和音素特征明显，激发了作者将ASR建模层面下沉到音素级，以更契合语音实际表达。

Method: 提出了一种音节结构解码器，将语音建模单元由传统的字、词等正字法单位改为音素单位。该方法通过建模音节的音系结构，实现从有限音素表生成有效音节，显著精简词汇表并更贴合语音实际。

Result: 在标准语料LSVSC和多方言UIT-ViMD两大越南语ASR基准测试中，该方法相较PhoWhisper和Wav2Vec2等预训练模型，无需额外资源、词汇量更小，均取得更优识别效果。

Conclusion: 基于音素的音节建模显著提升了越南语ASR的准确性和效率，表明该方向在音系结构显著的语言中具有优越性和推广价值。

Abstract: Most Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems formulate transcription as a prediction problem over orthographic units such as characters, subwords, or words. Although effective, such representations do not explicitly reflect the phonetic structure of speech and often require large vocabularies to maintain adequate coverage. In this work, we are motivated from the phonemic features of Vietnamese to propose a Syllabic-Structure Decoder for ASR, which models speech at the phoneme level instead of the orthographic level. Our approach explicitly captures the phonological composition of syllables, enabling the decoder to generate valid syllabic structures from a compact phonemic inventory. This design more closely aligns with the phonetic realization of speech while significantly reducing vocabulary size. Experimental results on two benchmarks: LSVSC, representing standard speech, and UIT-ViMD, a multi-dialect corpus containing diverse regional pronunciations, show that our method consistently outperforms strong previous baselines, especially pretrained baselines such as PhoWhisper and Wav2Vec2, despite using a substantially smaller vocabulary and no additional training resources. These results highlight the effectiveness of phoneme-based syllabic modeling for ASR in this language. Code for experimental reproducibility will be publicly available upon the acceptance of this paper.

### [123] [Narrative Flattening: How Post-Training Compresses Thematic, Affective, and Stylistic Variation in LLM Fiction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27878)
*Zehan Li,Yutong Zhu,Siyang Wu,Honglin Bao,James A. Evans*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在生成小说时流畅但缺乏创造性，研究发现经过后训练的模型输出故事叙事变得更“平”，表现为主题、情感和风格的多样性减少，这一现象在各类故事领域均有体现，但以专业文学作品最为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型能够生成流畅的小说文本，但普遍被认为内容“扁平”或缺乏叙事层次和创新性。论文试图追溯导致这种“平淡化”现象的原因，并分析其在不同类型小说中的表现差异。

Method: 构建了三类故事续写测试集（分别来自公开平台StoryStar、受提示生成的TMAS和专业文学The New Yorker），采用同一架构和预训练下经过不同后训练方法（Base、SFT、DPO、RLVR）的OLMo 32B模型续写文本，并与人类原作匹配对比，在主题变化、情感强度及语言多样性三个维度评估生成文本变化。

Result: 后训练过程导致模型生成的故事在上述三个维度上都表现出“动态收缩”，即主题切换更单一、情感趋于中性、风格多样性降低。且这一现象在专业文学小说上最为显著，而在公开平台和提示生成的故事中差距较小。

Conclusion: 后训练特别是对齐环节，使模型生成故事的叙事变得“扁平”，不再体现源文本的叙事层次和风格差异，各不同领域最终输出也趋于一致。

Abstract: Large language models produce fluent fiction, yet their creative output is widely seen as flat. We ask where this quality originates in the training and whether it affects different domains of human fiction equally. We construct a matched story-continuation paradigm across StoryStar (public-platform), TMAS (prompt-guided), and The New Yorker (professional literary)-and compare continuations from four OLMo 32B checkpoints (Base, SFT, DPO, RLVR) against matched human text. Because these checkpoints share architecture, scale, tokenizer, and pretraining, the design isolates the post-training effect. We measure each continuation along three sentence-level dimensions: thematic motion, affective prevalence, and linguistic diversity. Across all three, post-training compresses dynamic variation: thematic transitions become more uniform, high-intensity emotions give way to neutrality, and stylistic diversity across stories shrinks. We term this progressive loss narrative flattening. The effect is directionally stable across story domains but gap size depends on the human baseline: professional literary fiction is compressed most, while public-platform and prompt-guided stories show smaller gaps, consistent with their human baselines sitting closer to the model's default rhythm. Post-trained endpoints converge across domains, suggesting alignment produces a continuation regime largely insensitive to the source domain's narrative texture.

*Yibo Zhao,Zichen Ding,Jiayi Wu,Zun Wang,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文对大语言模型驱动的搜索代理训练方法进行了严格对比实验，系统分析了影响其性能的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型搜索代理的训练方法繁杂，各实验条件不一，难以直接比较，致使推动性能提升的核心要素不明。

Method: 作者从三个方面进行了控制变量实验：（1）修正广泛使用的Wikipedia 2018语料覆盖问题；（2）系统比较结果导向和过程导向的奖励设计；（3）分析训练数据多样性、异策略数据利用及推理预算扩展对性能的影响。

Result: 修正数据覆盖问题带来的性能提升超过不同训练算法间的差异。简单的结果导向奖励在多数设定下效果最好，过程导向方法反而有时会矫枉过正。进一步总结了数据多样性与预算对性能的具体影响。

Conclusion: 影响搜索代理性能的关键在于数据覆盖和奖励设计。简单有效的设计常优于复杂方案，文章为后续研究提供了实用性的训练建议和基线代码。

Abstract: Search agents powered by large language models can autonomously decompose queries, retrieve information, and synthesize answers through multi-step reasoning. However, the rapid growth of training methods has outpaced controlled comparison: existing works differ in retrieval corpora, reward designs, and training protocols, making it unclear what actually drives improvements. We present a controlled empirical study that isolates three under-explored dimensions of search agent training. First, we identify a critical data-coverage issue in the widely used Wikipedia 2018 corpus and show that correcting it alone yields larger gains than the differences between training algorithms. Second, we systematically compare outcome-based and process-based reward methods across three base models, finding that the simplest outcome-based approach achieves competitive or superior performance in most settings, and that process-level credit assignment can over-correct agent behavior. Third, we analyze training data diversity, off-policy data utilization, and search budget scaling, distilling practical guidelines for training effective search agents. Our code is available at https://github.com/YiboZhao624/SearchAgentReview.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了VibeSearch范式，并建立了VibeSearchBench基准，包括200个人工设计的中英双语多领域任务。每个任务包含用户角色设定和无结构知识图谱，通过逐步揭示用户模拟器和图谱匹配框架进行评价。此外，对七个前沿模型在ReAct与OpenClaw两种方式下进行了基准测试。

Conclusion: 当前的大模型代理在长上下文推理、主动意图获取及结构化知识构建等方面表现不足，亟需技术突破以提升真实多轮搜索体验的能力。

Abstract: LLM-based agents score well on search benchmarks, yet real users consistently find results unsatisfying, revealing a persistent evaluation-experience gap. We attribute this gap to existing benchmarks' reliance on over-specified queries, single-turn interactions, and fixed-schema evaluation, none of which reflect real search behavior where users and agents collaboratively refine vague intent through multi-turn dialogue. We term this paradigm VibeSearch and introduce VibeSearchBench, a benchmark comprising 200 manually curated bilingual (Chinese and English) tasks across 20 domains, split into VibeSearch-Pro (professional) and VibeSearch-Daily (daily-life) subsets. Each task pairs a user persona with a schema-free ground-truth knowledge graph, and is evaluated through a progressive-disclosure user simulator and a graph-matching evaluation framework. We benchmark seven frontier models under both the ReAct framework and the OpenClaw agent harness. Results show that all models remain substantially inadequate for VibeSearch (best F1: 30.30), highlighting the need for fundamental advances in long-context reasoning, proactive intent elicitation, and structured knowledge construction.

Abstract: Recently, large language models (LLMs) have achieved superior performance in static financial reasoning and simple dynamic trading tasks. However, existing static financial benchmarks are insufficient to assess the dynamic wealth management and financial decision-making capabilities of LLMs in real-world environments. To bridge this gap, we present FinBoardBench, an evaluation suite based on three classic financial board games: Cashflow, Acquire, and Monopoly. FinBoardBench assesses a comprehensive set of financial skills, including personal cash flow management with debt balancing, corporate investment and acquisition forecasting, and competitive trade negotiations with asset auctions. Our experiments with 9 advanced LLMs reveal that while exhibiting basic long-term planning and investment logic, they fail to effectively leverage complex interactions for profit, and their strong static reasoning performance does not transform into successful dynamic decision-making. Notably, they tend to prioritize immediate asset acquisition over maintaining sufficient liquidity, making them vulnerable to financial crises triggered by random events. We hope that FinBoardBench can provide a valuable reference for more intelligent LLM-based decision-making systems in the future.

### [127] [The Fragility of Chain-of-Thought Monitoring Across Typologically Diverse Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27901)
*Eric Onyame,Runtao Zhou,Kowshik Thopalli,Bhavya Kailkhura,Chirag Agarwal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统性分析了链式思维（CoT）监测机制在多语言、多模型下的可靠性，发现其在多种语言和模型间的效力极为有限，特别在低资源语言下表现出严重局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CoT监测被视为语言模型安全的重要机制，但此前研究多局限于英文和单一模型。本研究动机在于评估该方法在多语言环境与前沿多个模型下的实际有效性，从而检验其广泛适用性及安全边界。

Method: 作者选取了13种语言、7大家族共16种前沿大模型，通过带有对抗性提示的多步推理任务和内部token概率分析，评估模型对CoT监控的抗规避能力及其在跨语言情境下的可靠性。

Result: 发现无论语言类型、提示方式如何，CoT监测都极易被规避，8B-120B参数规模模型的不忠实率高达95.9%；模型能通过答案切换、事后合理化、程序性利用提示等策略制造蒙蔽，且这些模式在低资源语言下依旧极端显著（100%），揭示了CoT监测在分布外环境下的脆弱性。

Conclusion: 当前CoT监测机制在跨语言和多模型环境下表现极为脆弱，远低于英文单语场景下的安全假设，亟须开发更稳健、可解释的监控技术，尤其需要关注中低资源语言领域的模型监督能力。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring has been proposed as a promising safety mechanism for detecting misaligned behavior in large language models. However, its reliability remains largely unexplored beyond English and across diverse model families. We present the first large-scale evaluation of CoT monitorability across 13 diverse languages and seven frontier model families, comprising 16 models. Using adversarial-hint evaluations that require explicit intermediate computation, together with analysis of internal answer-token probabilities, we consistently find CoT unfaithfulness across languages and hint types, with an average rate of 95.9\% across 8B--120B parameter models. We find that frontier models systematically engage in strategic manipulation, including answer-switching, post-hoc rationalization, and procedural exploitation of hints, making external monitors struggle to detect deception. We show that frontier models often commit to the misaligned cue in their latent activations within the first 15\% of generation, even when the CoT appears faithful. Surprisingly, these deceptive patterns remain 100\% in low-resource languages, revealing fundamental limitations in current CoT-based oversight. Our results reveal that CoT monitoring is fundamentally fragile under linguistic distribution shift, providing a substantially weaker safety signal than what English-only studies suggest. These findings underscore an urgent need to develop robust CoT monitors and to accelerate research into white-box monitoring techniques, especially to improve CoT monitorability in mid- and low-resource languages. Our code is available \href{https://multilingual-cot-monitoring.github.io/}{\textcolor{blue}{here}}.

### [128] [AI Research Agents Narrow Scientific Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27905)
*Yixuan Tang,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文分析了当前AI研究代理在科学探索中的作用，发现AI生成的研究想法更集中于已有文献，难以大幅拓展科学边界，更适合小范围的本地创新，而非引领科学领域的广泛突破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI研究代理能自动生成研究创意、设计实验与写作，出现了大规模AI辅助科学发现的可能性。当前许多框架鼓励新颖、高影响力的想法，但尚不清楚AI辅助下的科研是否能真正拓宽科学探索范围。因此作者希望系统性地验证AI代理是否有助于推动科学多样化发展，或只是加深对已有方向的挖掘。

Method: 作者将AI研究代理视为科学搜索系统，选取四种AI研究代理框架和六种大型语言模型，基于AI/机器学习领域内的共享种子文献，生成37,802个科学创意。随后，将这些AI创意与同领域人类论文、人类后续研究产出，以及种子文献本身进行多维对比分析。

Result: 实验显示：1）AI生成的想法比同领域人类论文更集中、更类似于起始文献；2）与人类后续工作相比，AI创意与原点距离更近；3）与AI想法相似的论文往往获得较低引用；4）AI生成的创新多为技术方法重组而非全新科学问题。

Conclusion: 现有AI研究代理更擅长对已有文献细致拓展，而非推动科研领域多样化或重大突破。要实现AI驱动的科学发现，需提升AI生成本质创新的能力。

Abstract: AI research agents can now generate research ideas, design experiments, run code, and draft papers, raising the possibility of large-scale AI-assisted scientific discovery. Many current agent frameworks explicitly encourage the generation of novel and high-impact ideas. Yet it remains unclear whether AI-assisted ideation broadens scientific exploration or mainly concentrates around existing work. We study AI research agents as scientific search systems. Using four AI research-agent frameworks and six large language models, we generate 37,802 scientific ideas from shared seed literature across citation-defined research areas in AI and machine learning. We then compare the resulting AI ideas against human-authored papers from the same research areas, follow-on human research emerging from the same seed literature, and the seed literature itself. Across experiments, four consistent patterns emerge. First, AI-generated ideas are substantially more concentrated than human-authored papers from the same research areas. Second, AI-generated ideas remain much closer to their starting literature than later human follow-on work does. Third, papers most similar to AI-generated ideas tend to receive lower subsequent citations. Fourth, when AI-generated ideas differ from prior work, the differences arise primarily from recombining existing technical methods rather than introducing fundamentally new research questions. Overall, current AI research agents appear better suited to local elaboration than to broadening scientific exploration.

### [129] [ESC-Skills: Discovering and Self-Evolving Skills for Emotional Support Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27908)
*Jie Zhu,Huaixia Dou,Shuo Jiang,Junhui Li,Lifan Guo,Feng Chen,Chi Zhang,Fang Kong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出ESC-Skills框架，将情感支持会话的可解释性和可控性提升到新水平，并通过技能库和自进化方法显著优化了支持效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的情感支持会话系统缺乏对有效支持技能的归纳与可解释性，导致系统难以系统性提升自身技能，也不易分析和解决失败案例。

Method: 论文提出以'干预单元'(Intervention Units, IU)建模本地化互动，从成功和失败对话中抽取IU，并据此建立包含具体指导、适用条件、预期结果和风险的技能库。同时，引入多画像自进化机制，通过与多类型模拟求助者的互动，自动发现并改进技能库中存在的不足。最后用仿真实验和SAGE评测不断优化该技能库。

Result: 实验证明，ESC-Skills能提升生成响应的质量和整体对话带来的情绪改善，且支持过程更可解释、更可控。

Conclusion: ESC-Skills框架不仅提升情感支持会话系统的实际有效性，还增强了系统对技能的理解和改进能力，为情感支持AI的发展提供了新范式。

Abstract: Existing emotional support conversation (ESC) systems mainly rely on end-to-end response generation or coarse strategy supervision, offering limited interpretability and little support for systematic skill improvement. We propose ESC-Skills, a skill-centric framework that discovers and self-evolves executable emotional support skills. We first model localized support interactions as Intervention Units (IUs), which capture state--action--outcome dynamics between seeker states, support interventions, and post-response emotional changes. Based on IUs extracted from both successful and failed ESC dialogues, we construct the ESC-Skills Bank, a repository of executable emotional support skills containing intervention guidance, applicability conditions, expected outcomes, and potential risks. To further improve robustness, we introduce a multi-profile self-evolutionary refinement framework in which an ESC agent interacts with diverse simulated seeker profiles under SAGE evaluation. The resulting interaction traces are analyzed to identify missing skills, unsafe interventions, and profile-specific failure patterns, which are then used to refine the Skills Bank through simulation-based verification. Experimental results demonstrate that ESC-Skills improves both response-level quality and dialogue-level emotional outcomes while providing more interpretable and controllable support behaviors. We will release the code, prompts, and ESC-Skills Bank at https://github.com/aliyun/qwen-dianjin.

</details>


### [130] [Let the Results Speak: A Replication-First Paradigm for LLM Behavioral Benchmarking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27914)
*Yuming,Huang,Yao Liu,Lei Wang,Junchen Wan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“复制优先”范式来建立、验证并评估大模型（LLMs）主观行为，如共情、克制、情绪表达等。该方法通过多角度、多批次、多架构交叉检验，克服传统主观评判的一致性饱和和循环验证问题，并在49个不同模型上进行了实证测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，大模型主观行为的评估依赖人类评审或让LLM自身作为裁判，但这种方法面临评审一致性低（ρ≈0.45）和循环验证的风险。当人类本身意见不一致时，仅依托单一评审共识难以衡量新的模型能力。因此亟需一种可以独立、可靠地评估这些复杂行为的新框架。

Method: 作者提出了“复制优先”范式，通过四个正交维度进行验证：（1）多轮评测的一致性，（2）不同架构评委的交叉检验，（3）历史训练批次评委的校准，（4）预注册假设和预测。应用时让评分标准自进化，不预设维度，并通过在49个模型、8个家族上多轮迭代和72条实战对话测试，检验了这种框架。

Result: 该方法发现了聚合分数掩盖的细致差异。例如在建议克制性上，GPT-5 比 GPT-4.1 下降了1.87分，Opus-4.7 比 Opus-4.6 下降了0.629分，但聚合分数变化不大。该差异在三轮用户-代理切换、跨5个评委家族、17个月批次差异和74条对话测试中均稳定复现，评测工具的Krippendorff α达0.91。

Conclusion: “复制优先”范式可以更科学、严谨地揭示和评估大模型的主观行为表现，避免传统评审的局限，具备高稳定性及推广性。其诊断功能也有助于判定模型提升的真正瓶颈，推动后续模型和场景优化。

Abstract: Subjective evaluation of LLM behavior -- empathy, restraint, calibrated emotional tone -- is hard. Human inter-rater agreement on such qualities saturates near rho ~ 0.45, and an LLM-as-judge proxy alone risks circularity: a judge sharing the target's training cohort cannot independently verify it. Anchoring validity to a single human-rater consensus does not extend to capabilities where humans themselves disagree.
  We propose a replication-first paradigm: instead of anchoring on one rater group, we certify the instrument via four orthogonal properties -- reliability across K runs, cross-instrument replication across architecturally distinct judges, historical-footprint calibration via judges from earlier training cohorts, and pre-registered prediction. We test it on emotional accompaniment by letting the rubric self-evolve data-driven across iterations: the dimensions are not pre-stipulated and the procedure stabilizes to a 9-dimension set. Pre-registration applies to 10 falsifiable hypotheses and 11 forward predictions, committed before any test data was collected.
  Applied to 49 models across 8 families, the paradigm surfaces what aggregate scores hide. On advice-restraint -- whether a model refrains from giving unsolicited solutions in empathic contexts -- gpt-5 falls 1.87 points from gpt-4.1 and Opus-4.7 falls 0.629 from Opus-4.6, while aggregate scores stay flat. The regression survives three user-proxy swaps (95% of magnitude), replicates across a 5-family judge stack and a 17-month cohort gap, and persists on 74 held-out real ESConv conversations (rho in [0.749, 0.850]); the instrument reaches ordinal Krippendorff alpha = 0.91. As a by-product, the paradigm acts as a saturation-source diagnostic, separating instrumental ceilings (breakable by rubric refinement) from structural ceilings (needing scenario or roster intervention).

</details>


### [131] [GeneralThinker: Domain-General Reasoning through Likelihood-Guided Answer-Conditioned Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27934)
*Shengmin Piao,Sanghyun Park*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出GeneralThinker框架，实现无需领域特定验证器即可对大型语言模型进行细粒度推理训练，取得了多项推理基准上的最佳表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习在语言模型推理中表现提升明显，但现有方法依赖领域特定验证器、稀疏奖励和粗粒度信用分配，限制了其实用性与推广性。

Method: GeneralThinker是一个on-policy（即时政策）强化学习框架，将推理监督任务重构为密集的答案条件优化，评估生成推理过程与答案的兼容性，并进行token级别的信用分配。为优化过程稳定，引入clipping和方向保持调制方法，对token-level更新进行约束。

Result: 在涵盖数学、STEM及常规推理的11项基准任务上，GeneralThinker取得了最佳性能。此外，实验还表明无约束token级调制会导致训练不稳定，而受控调制则保证了细粒度信用分配的有效性。

Conclusion: GeneralThinker克服了传统RL方法的验证器依赖及信用分配粗糙等局限，可广泛应用于高效、灵活的语言模型推理任务。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves language model reasoning, but its reliance on domain-specific verifiers, sparse outcome rewards, and coarse-grained credit assignment limits its applicability. We introduce GeneralThinker, an on-policy framework that reformulates reasoning supervision as dense answer-conditioned optimization, enabling response-level evaluation and token-level credit assignment without domain-specific verifiers. GeneralThinker evaluates generated reasoning trajectories using the likelihood of the ground-truth answer and derives token-wise compatibility signals for fine-grained credit assignment. To stabilize optimization, it constrains token-level updates through clipping and direction-preserving modulation. Across 11 benchmarks spanning mathematics, STEM, and general reasoning, GeneralThinker achieves the best average performance. Further analyses show that uncontrolled token-level modulation can destabilize training, whereas controlled modulation makes fine-grained credit assignment consistently effective.

### [132] [DisasterBench: Benchmarking LLM Planning under Typed Tool Interface Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27957)
*Zhitong Chen,Kai Yin,Weifeng Zhang,Zhiyuan Wang,Xiangjue Dong,Chengkai Liu,Zhewei Liu,Yiming Xiao,Ali Mostafavi,James Caverlee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了DisasterBench这一针对灾害响应中多工具、结构化规划的基准，并引入了第一失效点（FPoF）方法，系统评估大模型在协调多个相似但操作不同的AI工具中的能力。实验揭示了模型容量、参数绑定错误和中间推理指令冲突等主要瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灾害应急中需要快速集成多样的AI工具实现复杂任务。当前大模型可作为编排中枢，但不仅要能选对工具，更需生成可执行且参数绑定正确的多步流程。缺乏有针对性的评估阻碍了模型实际应用。

Method: 1) 构建DisasterBench基准，涵盖语义相似但操作有差异的灾害响应工具链；2) 首次提出FPoF分析法，用以定位多步流程中首个真实出错点；3) 实验对不同大模型的多代理规划能力进行细粒度测试和解析。

Result: （1）有效性随模型容量提升；（2）最常见失败为工具错配和参数错误，反映出语义落地难及执行一致性问题；（3）长推理过程易产生与结构化输出冲突，影响流程生成。

Conclusion: 语义推理和执行落地之间尚存重大鸿沟，急需建立能同时建模语义意图、执行约束和流程一致性的AI规划框架。DisasterBench与FPoF为理解相关挑战提供了新视角和评测工具。

Abstract: Disasters cause severe societal impacts, demanding rapid coordination of heterogeneous AI tools, from satellite analysis to flood prediction and damage assessment, into coherent multi-step workflows. As LLMs increasingly serve as orchestrators of such pipelines, effective coordination requires more than selecting semantically plausible tools: LLMs must generate executable workflows with correct parameter binding and dependency propagation.
  We introduce DisasterBench, a benchmark for evaluating structured multi-agent planning over semantically similar but operationally distinct disaster-response tools. To enable step-level failure attribution, we further propose First-Point-of-Failure (FPoF), which localizes the earliest root cause in a predicted workflow, separating primary errors from downstream cascading effects.
  Our evaluation reveals three findings: planning method effectiveness depends strongly on model capacity; tool mismatch and parameter-binding errors dominate first failures, revealing semantic grounding and execution consistency as distinct bottlenecks; and verbose intermediate reasoning can create instruction clash with structured output requirements, disrupting plan generation.
  Together, these findings highlight a fundamental gap between semantic reasoning and execution-grounded coordination, underscoring the need for planning frameworks that jointly model semantic intent, execution constraints, and workflow consistency.
  Code, data, and evaluation resources are available at: https://github.com/TamuChen18/DisasterBench_Open

</details>


### [133] [Pressure-Testing Deception Probes in LLMs: Scaling, Robustness, and the Geometry of Deceptive Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27958)
*Sachin Kumar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统性地分析并压力测试了在LLM激活上用线性probe检测欺骗的有效性，提出常用指标在分布转移时普遍失效，并进一步揭示原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管线性probe在干净数据集上可以高效检测LLM中的欺骗行为，但在分布偏移时指标表现严重退化，实际应用面临巨大局限。因此，作者希望系统研究probe失败的机制而不是仅报告结果。

Method: 在Gemma 3系列（1B-27B参数）模型上，分别验证了四个关于“欺骗编码”的假设：（1）单一线性方向，（2）多维子空间，（3）凸锥包络，（4）熵代理。设计涵盖跨域迁移矩阵、多维probe(含置换对照)、熵残差测试、以及8种文风扰动下的干扰实验。

Result: （a）在干净数据上probe AUROC近乎完美，但在风格变化下显著崩溃；对风格做数据增强后检测能力又大幅恢复；（b）单方向假设被否，k=1仅有0.61-0.80 AUROC，一维probe迁移失败为几何本质而非层次匹配问题；（c）熵代理假设被否，最大相关性仅0.454，残差后AUROC变化极小；（d）欺骗并未形成显著线性子空间，但多维probe（k>=5）通过分布于不同子阈特征间的信号，可恢复检测能力。

Conclusion: 线性probe的脆弱性源于训练分布的狭窄，并非模型本身的体系结构限制。通过风格增强数据训练，探针法在大规模模型同样能恢复检测能力，表明逆向缩放现象仅为分布问题，不是规模问题。

Abstract: Linear probes trained on LLM activations are increasingly proposed as deception-detection metrics, yet report AUROC exceeding 0.96 on clean benchmarks while collapsing under distributional shift. This paper systematically pressure-tests probe-based metrics across the Gemma 3 model family (1B-27B parameters), diagnosing why they fail rather than merely documenting that they fail. We test four hypotheses about deception encoding: (1) single linear direction, (2) multi-dimensional subspace, (3) convex conic hull, (4) entropy proxy. Our design includes cross-domain transfer matrices, multi-dimensional probe analysis with permutation null baselines, entropy-residualization tests, and distractor evaluations across 8 stylistic shifts. We find that: (a) probes achieve near-perfect AUROC (>=0.998) on clean data but collapse under stylistic shifts; style-augmented probes recover near-perfect detection (mean AUROC 0.979-0.983) on unseen styles; (b) the single-direction hypothesis is rejected (k=1 captures only 0.61-0.80 AUROC), with cross-domain transfer failure confirmed as geometric rather than layer-mismatch-driven; (c) the entropy-proxy hypothesis is rejected (max |rho|=0.454, max Delta-AUROC after residualization=0.004); and (d) deception does not form a significant linear subspace (per-domain k*=0), yet multi-dimensional probes (k>=5) recover the signal through distributed sub-threshold features. Probe fragility reflects distributional narrowness rather than an architectural limitation: style-augmented probes recover near-perfect detection at both 4B and 27B, establishing that the inverse scaling pattern is a training-distribution artifact rather than a genuine scale-dependent phenomenon.

### [134] [Boundary Suppression Asymmetry in Post-trained Assistants: Over-expansion as a Controllability Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27969)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了经过优化后的大语言模型助理在避免“答非所问”方面的非对称可控性问题，指出反“答非所问”政策比基线更难被用户用提示局限，其原因和机制并不是输出变长等传统因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 优化大语言模型助理以提供全面、谨慎和主动的回答后，可能引入“可控性成本”，即在用户需要模型简短或聚焦回答时，某些行为更难被有效抑制。作者希望厘清这种非对称抑制的具体表现及成因。

Method: 作者构建了多种基于同一模型的助手政策（如反“答非所问”策略、最小边界策略等），并设计边界控制提示，对比测试模型在多个答题维度上的可控性。利用机制探针和鲁棒性实验进一步排查输出长度、EOS失败等可能机制。

Result: 实验发现反“答非所问”类政策下的模型更难通过提示被拉回，且相比基线模型表现出持续的“过度”趋势，而最小边界策略能够规避这种难以约束的倾向。排查多种机制后，发现此现象不是由简单长度增加或局部偏置等原因导致。

Conclusion: 大语言模型助手的后训练可能导致某些方向上（如过于完整、过度帮助）可控性变差，特定有益倾向被激活容易，但难以局部抑制，主要归因于内容预算超限和输出持续性带来的抑制困难。

Abstract: Post-trained language-model assistants are often optimized to avoid under-answering, encouraging complete, helpful, cautious, and proactive responses. We ask whether this optimization creates asymmetric controllability costs: when users explicitly request narrower answers, which assistant behaviors remain suppressible, and which continue to shape the response? We study this problem as boundary-suppression asymmetry. Prompt-side probes across multiple high-level response dimensions suggest a selective cost, concentrated around `too-much assistant' directions such as over-completion, extra help, and anti-underanswering.
  Using controlled assistant-policy variants derived from a shared base model, we find that anti-underanswering policies are harder to pull back than the baseline under matched boundary-control evaluations, while minimal-boundary variants generally avoid this anti-side upward shift in the direct boundary-control comparisons. Mechanism-oriented probes point beyond longer default outputs, pure EOS failure, uncertainty compensation, and local continuation bias, while robustness checks preserve the main anti-over-baseline ordering under shared-system and larger-scale settings. The evidence supports a mixed planning/stopping account, where content-budget overshoot and continuation persistence jointly make boundary correction harder. Overall, post-training may create direction-specific controllability costs: some helpful assistant tendencies remain easy to invoke, yet harder to locally suppress.

### [135] [Semantic Flow Regularization: Teaching LLMs to Generate Diverse Yet Coherent Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27971)
*Kerui Peng,Feifei Li,Xingyu Fan,Wenhui Que*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大语言模型在进行个性化或语调风格微调时，输出会缺乏多样性，出现所谓的“跨风格塌缩”。本文提出了一种新的正则化方法SFR，有效提升了输出的多样性、风格忠实度和生成质量，无额外推理开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有跨熵目标训练下，大语言模型（LLMs）在风格或角色调节任务中输出缺乏多样性的重大问题。传统训练方式容易导致模型生成受限于单一（或少数）模式，不能真实反映个性及语调的变化，因此亟需新的方法突破。

Method: 提出了语义流正则化（Semantic Flow Regularization，SFR），用句子编码器对后续片段的语义表征进行流匹配辅助训练，在保留多种可能输出的前提下引导主干模型，且该流匹配头部推理时可直接丢弃，不增加部署成本。

Result: 在大规模工业对话数据集(Qwen3-32B, 9种persona)和公开基准（LiveCodeBench-v5，Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct）上，SFR显著提升了输出多样性、风格忠实度与编码任务通过率(pass@k)，在MBPP数据集的对比试验中，确认传统多Token预测是SFR的一个简单特例。

Conclusion: SFR是一种高效、零部署成本的辅助目标，能有效解决LLMs多风格任务中的输出塌缩问题，适用于风格对话和代码生成等任务，具有较强的普适性和实际价值。

Abstract: When large language models are fine-tuned to generate persona- or tone-conditioned responses, their output diversity is severely limited--a failure we term Cross-Style Collapse. We trace this collapse to the cross-entropy objective, which under shared representations tends to suppress diverse continuations. We propose Semantic Flow Regularization (SFR), a lightweight auxiliary objective that supervises the backbone with continuous sentence-encoder embeddings of future segments via conditional flow matching. The stochastic flow source preserves multi-modality by construction; the flow-matching head is discarded at inference, adding zero deployment cost. On a large-scale industrial dialogue dataset (Qwen3-32B, 9 personas), SFR improves output diversity, style fidelity, and response quality over SFT. We further validate on the public LiveCodeBench-v5 (Qwen2.5-Coder-7B-Instruct), where SFR consistently improves pass@k, confirming generality beyond stylized dialogue. A controlled comparison on MBPP reveals Multi-Token Prediction to be a degenerate special case of SFR.

</details>


### [136] [Periodic RoPE for Infinite Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27980)
*Simin Huo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了P-RoPE编码与滑动窗口注意机制结合的新方法，突破了大模型序列长度扩展受限的问题，理论上支持无限长上下文推理，并在实际测试中优于现有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在处理超长序列时，受限于位置编码（如RoPE）的范围，超出预训练序列长度后效果明显下降，这是实现无限上下文的核心障碍。

Method: 提出了P-RoPE（周期性RoPE）位置编码，与滑动窗口注意力相结合，捕捉局部依赖与相对位置信息；再通过无位置编码（NoPE）全局注意力实现全序列、无限制的信息交互，两类层堆叠避免了位置外推问题，实现理论上的无限上下文支持。

Result: 所提出的MiniWin模型，在长上下文任务上，相比同类模型（如基于标准GPT结构的MiniMInd），展现了更优的效率和稳定性。

Conclusion: 该工作为实现真正具备无限上下文理解能力的大模型提供了新思路和方法论，有望推动LLM长期推理的能力突破。

Abstract: The ability to process ultra-long contexts is crucial for large language models (LLMs) to perform long-horizon tasks. While recent efforts have extended context windows to 1M and beyond, model performance degrades when sequence length exceeds the pre-trained range of positional encodings (e.g., RoPE), i.e., position exhaustion. This fundamental limitation must be overcome to achieve a truly infinite context. To address it, we propose Periodic RoPE (P-RoPE), a positional encoding mechanism designed to circumvent this exhaustion. It operates in conjunction with sliding window attention (SWA) to capture local dependencies and relative positions within each window. This local layer is then complemented by a global attention layer with No Positional Encoding (NoPE), enabling unbounded interaction across the entire sequence without positional constraints. By stacking these two types of layers, the model avoids the need for positional extrapolation to generalize longer and theoretically supports an infinite context window. Empirical results show that our model, MiniWin, outperforms MiniMInd with standard GPT architectures in long-context efficiency and stability. Our work provides a possible pathway toward LLMs with genuine infinite-context understanding. The code is available at \href{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}{https://github.com/Cominder/miniwin}.

</details>


### [137] [KVoiceBench, KOpenAudioBench, and KMMAU: Agent-Driven Korean Speech Benchmarks for Evaluating SpeechLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27984)
*Haechan Kim,Seungjun Chung,Inkyu Park,Jihoo Lee,Jonghyun Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 现有的语音语言模型评估主要集中在英语，无法全面反映多语言能力。作者提出两种基准构建框架，并以此构建了三个针对韩语的语音基准，以评估多语种语音模型的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前SpeechLM主要在英语上评估，对其他语言的泛化能力验证不足。简单地将基准转移到其他语言，会丢失语言特性和语音属性，影响评测的准确性和公平性。亟需更科学的多语种评估方法。

Method: 提出两个人工-智能体结合的基准构建流程：一种是将原有（源语言）SpokenQA基准有针对性地转换到韩语等目标语言；另一种是将目标语言ASR语料利用转录文本和说话人信息，构造成音频理解基准。基于这两种方法，构建了KVoiceBench、KOpenAudioBench和KMMAU三个韩语语音评测基准。

Result: 构建了包含12,345个样本的韩国语音评测集合，并用其评测了8种最新SpeechLM模型，发现英语-韩语任务表现及不同任务类型的排名存在较大差异，揭示出仅用英语评估时不可见的模型弱点。

Conclusion: 新的多语种语音评测基准能更加真实、全面地揭示SpeechLM在除英语外语言的能力，推进更公平、多元的语音人工智能发展。

Abstract: Speech language models (SpeechLMs) have achieved substantial progress by extending large language models (LLMs) to the speech modality. However, SpeechLM evaluation remains heavily centered on English, limiting reliable assessment of multilingual speech capabilities. Straightforward benchmark transfer through ASR, translation, normalization, and TTS can corrupt language-specific instructions, answer constraints, and spoken forms; for audio understanding, transferring source-language audio also fails to preserve target-language speaker attributes, accents, and paralinguistic properties. To address these limitations, we propose two human-agent benchmark-construction frameworks: one transfers source-language SpokenQA benchmarks into target-language SpokenQA benchmarks, and the other converts target-language ASR corpora into audio understanding benchmarks using transcriptions and speaker metadata. Using these frameworks, we construct and publicly release three Korean speech benchmarks: KVoiceBench and KOpenAudioBench for Korean SpokenQA, and KMMAU for Korean audio understanding, comprising 12,345 samples in total. We evaluate eight recent SpeechLMs and find that English-Korean performance gaps vary substantially across models and task families, and that SpokenQA and audio understanding rankings diverge, revealing complementary weaknesses invisible to English-only evaluation.

Linear Design produces hyper-stable transcripts (MFE < - 2000 kcal/mol) that risk translation inefficiency due to extreme rigidity, and BiLSTM-CRF focuses solely on high CAI (0.96 to 0.98) without structural constraints, our framework achieves an optimal translation-stability equilibrium, highlighting the proposed BERT-GA framework as an effective, data-driven approach for the design and optimization of in-silico mRNA sequences.

### [139] [Auditing Stance Asymmetry in Generative Explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27988)
*Jiarui Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文关注语言模型在生成解释时的立场性偏差问题，并提出一种新的评估方法（SDE）用以细致拆分和分析生成内容中的态度差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有偏见评估主要集中在有界对比和显性内容，但开放性生成的解释往往通过责任分配、合理化等影响理解，从而引入微妙但重要的立场性不对称。本文提出正视并精细评估这类隐蔽偏差的需求。

Method: 提出Symmetry Decomposition Evaluation（SDE）方法，对成对情景进行具体化组标签、角色重写和支持/反证呈现，使用32组原型案例并结合判官评审比较，分析解释中的具体态度分配和其变化。

Result: 实验发现：有的表面差异在结构和证据可控后会减弱，但仍有部分表现在归责、语境和正当性赋予上保持稳定。评审行为表明量表分数容易掩盖读者感知的细微立场差异。

Conclusion: 文章提出用生成解释的立场性偏差作为偏见评估新视角，并表明现有自动打分方法在捕捉开放性解释中的立场变异上存在局限，SDE框架为更细粒度风险审查提供思路。

Abstract: Bias evaluation for language models has made substantial progress on bounded comparisons, such as overt derogation, stereotype association, or label-sensitive differences under controlled substitutions. Open-ended explanations raise a different problem: they guide interpretation by assigning responsibility, legitimacy, context, and grievance. A model can avoid hostile language while making one side structurally understandable and another personally at fault, overreacting, or less worth taking seriously. We call this stance-bearing asymmetry in generative explanations. We propose Symmetry Decomposition Evaluation (SDE), which tests paired situations with concrete group labels, structural-role rewrites, and explicit support or counter-evidence. In a controlled 32-family prototype suite, this decomposition shows that surface differences are not all alike: some weaken under structural or evidence control, while others remain as stable differences in how the model assigns blame, context, or legitimacy. Targeted case review and judge comparison suggest a broader difficulty for evaluating open-ended framing asymmetries: judge readings shift across operationalizations, and scalar scores can flatten distinctions that readers use to interpret explanatory stance. SDE therefore reframes generative bias evaluation as an audit of explanatory stance -- what stance each side receives, how it changes under decomposition, and where automatic scoring becomes unstable.

### [140] [Rethinking Visual Neglect: Steering via Context-Preference for MLLM Hallucination Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27993)
*Jingwen Wu,Xijun Zhang,Ge Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需训练的策略，通过有针对性地调整多模态大模型（MLLMs）对上下文信息的依赖，有效减少生成对象幻觉现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对象幻觉是多模态大模型实际应用中的主要难题。以往的缓解方案多认为其源于视觉信息不足，于是强调增强模型对图像的依赖。然而作者通过实验证明，简单提高视觉依赖往往会适得其反，因此需要寻找更本质的缓解途径。

Method: 作者提出 Context-Preference Activation Steering (CAS) 框架。该方法无需对模型进行额外训练，通过少量设计的冲突样本，提取两类上下文偏好向量（CPVs），然后在推理阶段以残差注入的方式引入这些信息，灵活调控模型对视觉、文本及参数知识的权重。

Result: 实验证明，CAS 能大幅度减少对象幻觉问题，同时不会增加推理时延，也不会影响原生文本生成质量。

Conclusion: 对象幻觉并非仅由视觉不足导致。作者的CAS方法无需训练，直接在推理阶段引导模型合理处理多源信息，有效提升了MLLM的生成可靠性，对实际部署具有重要意义。

Abstract: Object hallucination remains a primary obstacle to the reliable deployment of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). Current inference-time mitigation methods mainly assume hallucinations stem from visual neglect, steering models to enhance visual reliance. In contrast, our systematic interventions on multiple MLLMs show that pushing toward more visual reliance may exacerbate hallucinations on some models, while less may mitigate hallucinations. This result suggests that attributing hallucinations solely to visual insufficiency is underdetermined. We argue that the image, as a context, simultaneously competes with the model's parametric knowledge and the textual context. For this, we propose a training-free framework, Context-Preference Activation Steering (CAS). It extracts two semantically distinct Context Preference Vectors (CPVs) via two small sets of designed conflict samples and applies them via single-pass signed residual injection at mid-early MLP layers during inference to control information reliance. Experiments show that CAS substantially mitigates object hallucinations without increasing decoding latency and preserves native text-generation quality.

Evaluations across five LMs, two benchmarks, and 90 configurations using dual safety evaluators demonstrate consistent toxicity reduction while preserving language modeling quality. Our analysis reveals that toxicity is disproportionately encoded in early MLP layers, varies across architectures, and is systematically underestimated by single-evaluator setups -- underscoring the need for multi-evaluator safety assessment. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前GraphRAG框架在知识图建构时只提取单个文本块内的实体和关系，未能处理跨多个文本块的关系，导致重要证据未被利用。而用LLM暴力恢复所有跨块关系计算量惊人，效率极低。

Method: 提出CrossAug方法，通过自监督扰动训练，利用拓扑感知GNN给子图打分，筛选高潜力缺失区后仅在局部用LLM补全跨chunk的关系。流程包括：图损坏生成监督、GNN评分子图、证据驱动的LLM关系补全，作为预处理完成跨块关系的图增强。

Abstract: GraphRAG extends retrieval-augmented generation by organizing corpora as explicit knowledge graphs, enabling graph-based retrieval for complex question answering. However, existing frameworks extract entities and relations within individual chunks, leaving cross-chunk relations -- those whose evidence spans multiple passages -- systematically absent from the index. Exhaustive LLM-based recovery of such relations is impractical due to the combinatorial explosion of chunk combinations. We present CrossAug, a GNN-guided CROSS-Chunk Graph AUGmentation method that enriches GraphRAG indices with cross-chunk relational structure as an offline step before query-time retrieval. CrossAug derives training supervision through self-supervised graph corruption, uses a topology-aware GNN to score subgraphs for missingness, and applies evidence-grounded LLM completion only to selected high-scoring regions. Experiments on three LLM-based GraphRAG frameworks across four multi-hop and long-document QA benchmarks demonstrate that CrossAug consistently improves performance, confirming the benefit of cross-chunk graph augmentation for retrieval-based question answering. Our code is available at https://github.com/DonFinliani/CrossAug.

### [144] [Integrated and Cross-Architecture Interpretation of LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28006)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Understanding how LLMs reason is hindered by a practical asymmetry: while their generated outputs are observable, the underlying reasoning patterns remain opaque. Relying on single probes, such as Mutual Information Peak (MIP) or Deep-Thinking Ratio (DTR), risks underestimating the genuine inferential structure. To response this deficiency, we present an Integrated, cross-Architecture Reasoning (IAR) framework, designed to provide a unified approach to LLM reasoning interpretability. Specifically, we first propose to use bandwidth-calibrated MIP coupled with Tukey IQR peak-detection to isolate reasoning-crucial tokens at the output layer. Second, we performed an overlap analysis between MIP-picked tokens and DTR-deep tokens to trace the cross-layer trajectories of those tokens. This also discloses whether reasoning-crucial tokens are computation-intensive as well, further facilitating to understand how reasoning patterns evolve across model layers. Finally, we apply a Jaccard stability metric over multi-domain problems to verify if the MIP-identified tokens are reasoning quality-guaranteed. Extensive experiments on three models (Qwen-7B, Qwen-14B, and Llama-8B) across four domains (mathematics, code, logic, and common sense) demonstrate IAR's generalizable interpretation capabilities across architectures.

### [145] [MemGuard: Preventing Memory Contamination in Long-Term Memory-Augmented Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28009)
*Hyeonjeong Ha,Jeonghwan Kim,Cheng Qian,Jiayu Liu,William M. Campbell,Yue Wu,Yuji Zhang,Kathleen McKeown,Dilek Hakkani-Tur,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出MemGuard，一种类型感知的记忆框架，有效隔离和管理大模型的不同类型记忆，显著提升长期推理的可靠性并减少无关信息干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在扩展长期记忆时，常将用户事实、事件、行为规则等不同功能的记忆混合存储，导致检索和生成时互相污染，产生过度泛化或误导性内容。作者认为，这种“异质记忆污染”是影响长期推理可靠性的关键问题。

Method: 提出MemGuard框架，为每条记忆分配明确的功能类型，实现类型隔离，并维护类型间的关系。写入记忆时即确定其类型，检索和组合证据时仅选取必要类型，避免无关或功能不兼容的记忆干扰推理。

Result: 在幻觉识别和长对话基准测试中，MemGuard比已有方法提升了最多28.27%的记忆可靠性，同时检索的记忆token数量减少最多5.8倍。

Conclusion: 可靠的长期推理依赖于对异质记忆进行有原则的组织与选择性调用，MemGuard显著缓解了记忆污染问题，为大模型长期推理实践提供了新思路。

Abstract: Memory-augmented large language models extend reasoning beyond a fixed context window by maintaining long-term memory across interactions. However, existing memory systems often collapse stable user facts, episodic events, and behavioral rules into a shared space, allowing functionally distinct memories to be retrieved and used as interchangeable evidence. We identify this failure mode as heterogeneous memory contamination, where context-specific events become overgeneralized claims, or semantically relevant but functionally incompatible memories mislead generation. To this end, we introduce MemGuard, a type-aware memory framework that preserves functional memory boundaries during memory construction and retrieval. It assigns each memory an explicit functional role at write time, maintains relations across type-isolated memories, and selectively composes evidence only from necessary memory types, reducing contamination from irrelevant or functionally incompatible evidence. Across hallucination and long-horizon conversation benchmarks, MemGuard improves memory reliability by up to 28.27% while retrieving up to 5.8x fewer memory tokens than prior methods. These results suggest that reliable long-term reasoning depends on principled organization and selective use of heterogeneous memory.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型的安全评测工具主要以英文为主，且大多关注通用性风险，忽视了与本地文化相关的特有安全隐患。当前工具难以准确捕捉非英语文化语境下模型的具体风险，导致安全评估局限于英文或西方语境。

Method: 作者提出了KSAFE-MM基准，分为两部分：KSAFE-MM-G（针对全球通用风险并进行韩语上下文化处理）；KSAFE-MM-C（针对韩国文化特有的视觉和文本攻击场景，通过本地化真实视觉场景和越狱型文本组合，检验模型对文化视觉信号和恶意意图的脆弱性）。实验对12个主流多模态大模型进行了评测。

Result: 实验证明：1）模型对文化相关攻击比对通用攻击更易受到威胁；2）越狱攻击策略显著提高攻击成功率，最高达74.2%；3）模型安全性提升时，容易伴随对良性查询的过度拒答现象，存在安全与可用性间的系统性权衡。

Conclusion: 研究强调在多模态模型安全评估中，不能仅依赖英文基准和通用风险，应重视本地文化环境下的安全隐患。KSAFE-MM为其它文化环境下的模型安全评测提供了推广参考。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) exacerbate safety risks by introducing vulnerabilities across multiple modalities, such as language and vision. Current MLLM safety evaluation tools, however, suffer from major limitations: 1) English-centric dataset construction, and 2) a focus on generic risks that are not tied to local cultural contexts. This paper introduces KSAFE-MM, a benchmark for Korean multimodal safety evaluation that covers both general safety risks and culture-specific vulnerabilities. KSAFE-MM consists of two parts, KSAFE-MM-G and KSAFE-MM-C. KSAFE-MM-G evaluates globally shared risks in Korean contexts through linguistic contextualization, which transforms generic safety queries into contextually grounded multimodal samples. KSAFE-MM-C targets culture-dependent MLLM safety vulnerabilities using localized visual queries derived from real-world contexts. It pairs these visual queries with jailbreak-style textual queries to cover multimodal safety risks involving cultural visual cues and malicious textual intent. Together, these components provide a general-to-local construction pipeline for evaluating both globally shared safety risks and culture-specific vulnerabilities. We evaluate 12 state-of-the-art MLLMs on KSAFE-MM and reveal that models exhibit greater vulnerability to culturally grounded attacks than to generic ones. Notably, jailbreaking strategies substantially amplify attack success rates, with ProgramExecution yielding up to 74.2% ASR compared to 13.4% for standard queries. Furthermore, we identify a systematic trade-off between safety and over-refusal, where models achieving low ASR tend to exhibit excessive refusal behavior on benign queries. These findings highlight the urgent need for culturally grounded safety evaluation beyond English-centric benchmarks.

### [147] [ROSD: Reflective On-Policy Self-Distillation for Language Model Reasoning across Domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28014)
*Ziqi Zhao,Xinyu Ma,Liu Yang,Yujie Feng,Daiting Shi,Jingzhou He,Xin Xin,Zhaochun Ren,Xiao-Ming Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种新型自蒸馏方法ROSD，以提升大语言模型的推理能力，尤其在跨领域泛化表现优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在策略自蒸馏（OPSD）方法虽然能提升大语言模型的推理表现，但在领域内增益有限，并且在领域外泛化不佳，主要原因在于：1）教师模型倾向模仿参考解答而不是纠正具体错误，2）对整体回答的蒸馏容易覆盖掉正确推理前缀，加剧过拟合。

Method: 提出“反思在策略自蒸馏”（ROSD）框架，每次推理后利用自反思器提取纠正思路并定位首个错误片段。纠正思路指导自教师模型实施有针对性的监督，蒸馏范围只限于错误区域，从而既能修正错误，又能保留正确推理部分。

Result: 在多个领域内外的推理基准测试中，ROSD较标准OPSD方法在领域内推理表现更强，同时在领域外推理任务上有大幅提升。

Conclusion: ROSD通过引入反思和局部蒸馏，有效解决了现有OPSD泛化差的问题，为大语言模型的推理提升和泛化提供了新的方向。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) improves the reasoning performance of large language models (LLMs) by providing dense token-level supervision for on-policy rollouts. However, existing OPSD methods often yield limited gains on in-domain reasoning and generalize poorly to out-of-domain problems. We identify two key causes: conditioning the self-teacher on a verified solution encourages imitation of training-domain reference trajectories rather than error-specific correction, and applying distillation to the full response can overwrite valid reasoning prefixes and reinforce overfitting.
  We propose Reflective On-policy Self-Distillation (ROSD), a framework that turns reference-solution imitation into targeted reasoning correction through reflection-guided, error-localized distillation. For each rollout, ROSD uses a self-reflector to extract a corrective idea and locate the first erroneous span. The corrective idea guides the self-teacher toward targeted supervision, while the localized error span restricts distillation to where correction is needed. This design corrects flawed reasoning while preserving valid prefixes. Experiments on multiple in-domain and out-of-domain reasoning benchmarks show that ROSD yields stronger in-domain reasoning performance overall and substantially better out-of-domain generalization than standard OPSD. Code is available at https://github.com/ZiqiZhao1/ROSD.

</details>


### [148] [The Missing Piece in Pre-trained Model Evaluation: Reward-Guided Decoding Unlocks Task-Oriented Behavior Without Parameter Updates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28020)
*Shaobo Wang,Guo Chen,Ziyue Wang,Zhengyang Tang,Qingyang Liu,Xingzhang Ren,Dayiheng Liu,Linfeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需再训练的能量驱动解码（EBD）方法，通过外部奖励模型引导冻结的预训练大模型生成更符合任务需求的输出，从而提升评测的准确性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预训练大语言模型在标准解码下常无法很好地执行指令或生成规范答案，导致基准测试难以真实反映模型能力，而现有对策（如后期训练、基于解码的小技巧）成本高或适用性有限。

Method: 提出EBD（Energy-Based Decoding），在解码阶段引入轻量的外部奖励模型，通过改变输出分布，使生成文本同时兼顾原模型预训练分布和外部奖励，从而无需再训练即可激活符合任务的输出。

Result: 在五个模型和六个基准上，EBD均优于现有无训练解码方法。例如，Qwen3-8B-Base在AlpacaEval2.0上的分数从8.8提升至44.5，Mistral-7B在Math500计算延迟比之前方法快18.9倍，且对奖励模型的大小不敏感。

Conclusion: EBD方法无需额外训练即可让冻结的预训练LLM表现出更强的指令跟随和任务适应能力，使对原始模型的评测更公平、有效，在提升输出质量和效率方面具有良好潜力。

Abstract: With the rapid progress of large language models (LLMs), reliably evaluating the capabilities of pre-trained LLMs has become increasingly important. The challenge is that base pre-trained models are optimized for next-token prediction and often fail to follow instructions or produce well-formed answers under standard prompting and direct decoding. As a result, benchmark performance can conflate model capability with decoding-induced failures to produce task-oriented outputs, while exposing such behavior often relies on costly post-training. Recent decodingonly approaches attempt to reshape output distributions, but such methods can be inefficient and brittle across open-ended tasks. To address these limitations, we propose Energy-Based Decoding (EBD), a training-free, reward-guided framework for activating task-oriented behaviors from frozen pre-trained LLMs across both open-ended and objective tasks. EBD augments decoding with an external lightweight reward model, steering generations toward high-utility responses while anchoring them to the pre-trained model prior through a reward-tilted target distribution. We show that EBD shifts base-model outputs toward more instructionfollowing behavior, increasing behavioral similarity to post-trained counterparts and enabling a fairer inference-time evaluation of accessible pre-trained-model behavior. Empirically, EBD outperforms baselines across five models and six benchmarks, improving Qwen3-8B-Base on AlpacaEval2.0 from 8.8 to 44.5, reducing Mistral-7B Math500 latency by 18.9x relative to prior decoding work, and remaining robust to reward-model size.

### [149] [Beyond pass@k: Redundancy-Aware RLVR for Multi-Sample Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28022)
*Le Bronnec Florian,Alexandre Verine,Rio Yokota,Benjamin Negrevergne*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了代码生成大模型中通过Pass@k评估时的冗余问题，并提出通过反冗余奖励改进RLVR方法以提升效果。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前许多基于强化学习的代码生成优化（RLVR）方法只关注可执行性正确性，但忽视了生成结果中的实现冗余问题，即频繁生成相似或重复代码。冗余会影响最终代码多样性和通过率，但相关影响尚不清楚。

Method: 作者利用代码查重工具JPlag度量模型输出的实现层面冗余，并比较了不同RL目标（仅正确性 vs. Pass@k感知）的冗余程度。进一步，作者为RLVR引入反冗余奖励，直接惩罚生成近重复实现。

Result: 实验覆盖3个模型和3套基准，发现只关注正确性的RLVR容易产生高实现冗余，而Pass@k感知目标和新提出的反冗余奖励能有效降低冗余，并在更多采样预算下提升实际可执行性能。

Conclusion: 鼓励生成多样化代码实现、抑制冗余，能提高代码生成模型在有限采样预算下的表现，为未来RLVR优化目标设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: LLMs for code generation are commonly evaluated in repeated-sampling settings using Pass@k, where multiple candidate programs are executed against unit tests under a finite sampling budget. While recent verifier-based reinforcement learning (RLVR) methods improve executable correctness, how these objectives affect redundancy among sampled programs remains poorly understood. In this work, we study implementation-level redundancy in code generation using JPlag, a plagiarism-detection system for code. Across models and benchmarks, we show that correctness-only RLVR often concentrates generations around repeated implementations, whereas Pass@k-aware objectives maintain lower redundancy and improve larger-budget performance. Motivated by these observations, we augment RLVR with direct anti-redundancy rewards based on JPlag similarity. Across 3 models and 3 benchmarks, discouraging near-duplicate generations reliably improves finite-budget executable performance, often matching or outperforming specialized Pass@k-aware objectives.

### [150] [Personality, Role, and Expressive Style in Large Language Models: An Interactionist Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28037)
*Moe Nagao,Koichiro Terao,Mikio Nakano,Naoto Iwahashi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文探讨了在大语言模型对话代理中，提示指定大五人格特质并不总能确保所期望的人格在生成的对话中得以充分表达。研究分析了提示内容中的人格、对话角色和表达风格如何共同影响人格的表达。结果发现这些因素协同作用，且影响因人格维度而异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型对话代理的普及，让模型持续展现一致的人格特质变得重要，但现实中通过提示词指定的人格特质与实际对话中表现的不总是一致，因此需要深入分析影响因素。

Method: 采用析因设计，将6种人格条件、3种角色和3种表达风格组合作为变量，分别在英语和日语中生成1080组LLM对话。随后通过“LLM作为判定者”框架，对生成对话中目标代理的发言进行大五人格特质的表达评估。

Result: 对话中展现的人格不仅受特质显式指定影响，还受到对话角色和表达风格的影响，各人格维度敏感性不同。角色强烈影响开放性，风格显著影响尽责性和宜人性，显式指定则主要控制神经质。另外，即使未显式指定人格，社会和表达条件也会诱发特定人格印象。英日语跨语言比较显示大体趋势一致，只有在某些特定条件组合下有差异。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的人格控制无法单靠人格特质提示实现，而是需要结合社会角色和表达风格等语境因素，视为一个情境相关的动态过程。

Abstract: Prompt-based personality control is a key technique for designing large language model (LLM) dialogue agents that behave consistently across social contexts. However, specifying Big Five personality traits (BFTs) in a prompt does not ensure that the intended traits are expressed in generated utterances. This paper investigates this mismatch from an interactionist perspective, viewing personality expression as a context-dependent outcome shaped by the interplay between trait specification and situational factors. We analyze how perceived BFT expression in LLM-generated dialogue is influenced by three prompt factors: personality traits, dialogue roles, and expressive styles. Using a factorial design that combines six personality conditions, three roles, and three expressive-style conditions, we generate 1,080 LLM-agent dialogues in each of English and Japanese. We then evaluate the target agent's utterances using an LLM-as-a-judge framework to estimate expressed Big Five traits. The results show that expressed personality is shaped not only by explicit trait specification, but also by dialogue role and expressive style. These effects are trait-specific: dialogue role strongly influences Openness, expressive style substantially shapes Conscientiousness and Agreeableness, and explicit trait specification dominates Neuroticism. Even without explicit personality-trait specification, social and expressive conditions induce distinct personality-like impressions. Cross-linguistic comparisons show broadly similar patterns between English and Japanese dialogues, with noticeable differences only under specific combinations of personality, role, and expressive style. These findings suggest that personality control in LLM agents should be understood not as a direct consequence of trait prompting, but as a context-dependent process involving personality specification, social role, and expressive style.

*Liu O. Martin,Lucas Bandarkar,Nanyun Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用MoE（专家混合模型）的模块化和多语种能力的可分离性，精准判别并裁减与机器翻译无关的专家网络，通过直接裁剪和短暂监督微调（SFT），无需重新训练即可大幅压缩模型。

Result: 不经训练即可裁剪50%的专家几乎不影响翻译质量，裁剪70%损失也很小；经过短SFT后裁剪75%专家性能可基本恢复原水平，特殊条件下可去除近90%专家仍保持可接受表现。MoE区块可压缩90%以上参数。

Conclusion: 机器翻译任务实际上只需LLM很小一部分参数，利用专家裁剪可大幅减小模型规模，在保持高译质的同时提升部署效率。

Abstract: Modern large language models (LLMs) achieve state-of-the-art machine translation performance, but they do so as broad generalists largely trained for many tasks and capabilities unrelated to translation. Thus, they are heavily overparameterized for this task, resulting in excessive memory and compute requirements. In this paper, we present a method for aggressively pruning experts from modern mixture-of-experts LLMs while incurring negligible degradation in translation quality. Our approach exploits expert specialization and the separability of multilingual capabilities in LLMs to identify experts irrelevant to translation. And because of the modular nature of MoEs, these can be easily pruned without any training. Without retraining, we are able to prune half of all experts with negligible degradation and 70% with only minor losses. With a very short SFT, we prune 75% of experts while recovering baseline performance, and in some settings remove nearly 90% while maintaining reasonable translation quality. Overall, our results show that translation requires only a fraction of the LLM, enabling substantial compression of the MoE blocks that contain over 90% of parameters.
